6) Using only "ls" (and maybe "grep"), can you find out which file under
    directory /proc/ contains information about memory (mem) on your
    server? Which file contains information about the cpu's on your server?
meminfo contains information about memory
cpuinfo contains information on the cpu's

    How many processors are on your server?  1

10) Search in the Tweets hashtags file for the case-insensitive
    word "great" (i.e. "Great" or "GREAT" also count). How many hashtags
    contain this word? You can use grep (case-insensitive) and wc.
114
 
11) Now use the file command to check the character encoding of the dataset. What character encoding does it have?
UTF-8 Unicode text
 
12) Now use the iconv  (or another) command to convert the tweet file to ascii character encoding. Search to read about ascii vs non-ascii encodings.
iconv -f utf-8 -t ascii
